

Q: abstract 
A: <p><strong>abstract </strong>[ˈæbstrækt] [同] theoretical [反] concrete</p><p><emphasis>adj. </emphasis>based on general ideas or principles rather than specific examples or real events 抽象的</p><p>The research shows that pre-school children are capable of thinking in <strong><emphasis>abstract</emphasis></strong> terms. 研究表明学龄前儿童有抽象思维能力。</p><p><emphasis>n. </emphasis>a short written statement containing only the most important ideas in a speech, article, etc. 摘要；概要</p>

Q: abundance 
A: <p><strong>abundance </strong>[əˈbʌndəns] [同] sufficiency [反] lack</p><p><emphasis>n. </emphasis>a large quantity of something 大量，充足</p><p>There is an <strong><emphasis>abundance</emphasis></strong> of evidence to support the research findings. 有大量的证据来支持研究结果。</p>

Q: abuse 
A: <p><strong>abuse </strong>[同]① misapply, make ill use of ② ill-treat</p><p>① <emphasis>v. </emphasis>[əˈbjuːz] to deliberately use something for the wrong purpose or for your own advantage 滥用</p><p>Biometrics raises thorny questions about privacy and the potential for <strong><emphasis>abuse</emphasis></strong>. 生物测定学引发了关于隐私以及该学科有可能被滥用等棘手问题。</p><p>② <emphasis>n. </emphasis>[əˈbjuːs] cruel or violent treatment of someone 虐待</p><p>Child <strong><emphasis>abuse</emphasis></strong> is a worldwide problem affecting children from birth to 18 years of age. 儿童虐待是个影响从刚出生到18岁之间儿童的全球性问题。</p>

Q: baggage 
A: <p><strong>baggage </strong>[ˈbægɪdʒ]</p><empty-line /><p><emphasis>n. </emphasis>(esp. AmE) the cases, bags, boxes, etc. carried by sb. who is traveling (=luggage) 行李</p><p>When you arrive at an airport in Australia, you may be greeted in the <strong><emphasis>baggage</emphasis></strong> hall by a detector dog, wearing a little red coat bearing the words 'Quarantine'. 当你到达澳大利亚的机场时，你会在行李大厅遇到穿着印有“检疫”字样红外套的稽查犬。</p>

Q: candidate 
A: <p><strong>candidate </strong>[ˈkændɪdeɪt] [同] applicant, seeker</p><p><emphasis>n. </emphasis>a person who is trying to be elected or is applying for a job（竞选或求职的）候选人，申请人</p><p>If a woman <strong><emphasis>candidate</emphasis></strong> manages to get on a shortlist, then she has probably already proved herself to be an exceptional <strong><emphasis>candidate</emphasis></strong>. 如果一位女候选人能进入最后的角逐，就已经证明她是个很出色的候选人了。</p>

Q: canteen 
A: <p></p><empty-line /><p><strong>canteen </strong>[kænˈtiːn]</p><empty-line /><p><emphasis>n. </emphasis>a place where food and drink are served in a factory, a school, etc. 食堂，餐厅</p><p>The <strong><emphasis>canteen</emphasis></strong> was absolutely packed and I had to wait for ages. 食堂里人满为患，我得等上好长时间。</p>

Q: capable 
A: <p><strong>capable </strong>[ˈkeɪpəbl] [同] able, competent [反] incapable</p><p><emphasis>adj. </emphasis>having the ability or qualities necessary for doing sth. 有能力的，有才能的</p><p>Even very tiny babies are <strong><emphasis>capable</emphasis></strong> of grasping and remembering a concept. 即使是很小的孩子也能领会和记住一个概念。</p>

Q: capacity 
A: <p><strong>capacity </strong>[kəˈpæsəti] [同] ability</p><p><emphasis>n. </emphasis>① the amount of space a container, room, etc. has to hold things or people 容量 ② the ability to do sth. 能力</p><p>The <strong><emphasis>capacity</emphasis></strong> of the environment to sustain economic development and population is finite. 环境承受经济的发展和人口的能力是有限的。</p>

Q: capital 
A: <p><strong>capital </strong>[ˈkæpɪtl]</p><empty-line /><p><emphasis>n. </emphasis>a large amount of money that is invested or is used to start a business 资本；资金</p><p>Cheap labour may make Chinese clothing competitive in America, but if delays in shipment tie up working <strong><emphasis>capital </emphasis></strong>and cause winter coats to arrive in spring, trade may lose its advantages. 廉价劳动力可能会让中国的服装产品在美国富有竞争力，但如果运货过程中的耽搁套牢了营运资金并导致冬装在春天才运送到，那服装贸易就没什么优势可言了。</p>

Q: data 
A: <p><strong>data </strong>[ˈdeɪtə]</p><empty-line /><p><emphasis>n. </emphasis>facts or information used in deciding or discussing sth. 资料，数据</p><p>Very little <strong><emphasis>data</emphasis></strong> is available. 现有的资料十分不足。</p>

Q: date 
A: <p><strong>date </strong>[ˈdeɪt]</p><empty-line /><p>① <emphasis>n. </emphasis>specific numbered day of the month, or specific year, usu. given to show when sth. happened or is to happen 日期；日子；年份</p><p>Times change, and one of the most significant changes to <strong><emphasis>date</emphasis></strong> is the rise of globalization. 时代在变，全球化的兴起成为迄今为止最为显著的变化之一。</p><p>② <emphasis>v. </emphasis>to have existed since a particular time in the past 存在，追溯</p><p>The first weather stations in the far north <strong><emphasis>date</emphasis></strong> back just 50 years. 在（地球）最北边的最早的气象站也不过存在了50年之久。</p>

Q: economy

Q: edition

(as being the specified person or thing) 确认、证明某人或某事物；鉴别出（系某人或某物）</p><p><strong><emphasis>Identifying</emphasis></strong> genetically talented individuals is only the first step. 鉴别出天生有才能的个体仅仅是第一步。</p>

A: <p><strong>whereas </strong>[ˌweərˈæz] [同] though</p><p><emphasis>conj. </emphasis>used to compare or contract two facts（用以比较或对比两个事实）然而；尽管；但是</p><p>Some of the studies show positive results, <strong><emphasis>whereas</emphasis></strong> others do not. 有一些研究结果令人满意，然而另一些则不然。</p>

Q: whereby

Q: assemble

Q: particular

Q: furnish

Q: furniture
